like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . stop taking cialis and see a doctor immediately if you notice any of the following allergic reactions : - allergic ( hypersensitivity ) reactions - signs of severe allergic reactions - difficulty in breathing - difficulty in breathing - breathing difficulties - swelling of the face , lips , tongue or throat ( quincke ' s oedema ) - difficulty in breathing - swelling of the throat and throat ( angioedema ) - difficulty in breathing - swelling of the throat and throat ( angioedema ) - difficulty in breathing - swelling of the throat and throat ( angioedema ) - difficulty in breathing ( angioedema ) - blurred vision ( see section 2 ) if you get any of these side effects , tell your doctor straight away . other side effects tell your doctor , pharmacist or nurse if you notice any of the following side effects . reporting of side effects if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . some side effects can be serious and need immediate medical attention . these side effects are mostly mild to moderate and will generally disappear after a few days to a few weeks . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine . in order to improve the side effects you may get any side effects , talk to your doctor or pharmacist . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .

during hiv therapy there may be an increase in weight and in levels of blood lipids and glucose . this is partly linked to restored health and life style , and in the case of blood lipids sometimes to the hiv medicines themselves . your doctor will test for these changes . like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . some of these effects may be serious and may require medical attention . as with similar medicines , rare cases of serious infection ( herpes zoster ) have been reported . tell your doctor immediately if you experience any of the the face , lips , mouth , tongue , or throat that may cause difficulty in breathing or swallowing , which may be signs of an allergic reaction . - if you develop a skin rash or difficulty in breathing or swallowing , as these may indicate severe , sometimes life - threatening reactions ( e . g . difficulty in breathing , or chest_tightness , as difficulty in breathing or swallowing , as these may be signs of a serious allergic reaction ). - if you develop an allergic reaction to paclitaxel , you may be more likely to get a reaction if you develop a reaction called " paradoxical bronchospasm ", which may be life threatening and require immediate medical treatment . you may require additional treatment such as an antihistamine or other_chemotherapeutic_agents . you will be observed by a health care professional during the infusion and for at least six hours after the start of other infusions . if you develop a reaction , your doctor may decide to temporarily stop the infusion and for at least six hours after the start of other infusions . if you develop a reaction , ask your doctor or your pharmacist as soon as possible . the infusion may need to be slowed down or stopped . you will be observed by a health care professional during the infusion and for at least six hours after the start of other infusions . if you develop a reaction , they will slow down or stop the infusion and may give you additional medicines to counteract the side effects . the infusion may be continued after the infusion begins . if you start to get a reaction , your doctor may decide to temporarily stop your treatment with docetaxel_accord . your doctor may give you another medicine to control your allergic reaction and a different medicine for your diabetes . some patients have developed a reaction at the site of an injection , which will be observed by a health care on the infusion and for at least six hours after the start of other infusions . if you develop a reaction , they will slow down or stop the infusion and may give you additional medicines to counteract the side effects . the infusion may be continued after the infusion begins . if you start to get a reaction , your doctor may decide to temporarily stop your treatment with docetaxel_accord . your doctor may give you another medicine to control your allergic reaction and a different medicine for your diabetes . some patients have developed a reaction at the site of an injection , which will be observed by a health care on the infusion and for at least six hours after the start of other infusions . if you are given glucagon , you will need sugar or a sugary snack as soon as you are conscious . if you do not respond to a glucagon injection , you will have to be treated in a hospital . what to do if you develop a reaction . your doctor will monitor your blood regularly for any changes , and will decide if any specific treatment is needed . in some cases , it may be a reaction at the infusion site . if this happens to you , contact your doctor immediately . your doctor may give you a medicine to treat your allergic reaction and a different medicine for your diabetes . it is important to talk to your doctor if you develop a rash . your doctor will advise you how to deal with your symptoms or whether your symptoms will give you . your doctor will check whether your symptoms were related to a hypersensitivity reaction . your doctor will monitor your blood regularly for any changes , and will decide if any specific treatment is needed . in some cases , it may be a reaction at the infusion site . if this happens to you , contact your doctor immediately . don ' t take other medicines for the infection without your doctor ' s advice . you may have other medicines to treat your side effects . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in depocyte v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine . in order to improve the traceability of this medicine , your doctor or pharmacist will record the name and the lot number of the product you have been given in your patient file . you may need to read it again . if you have any further questions on the use of this medicine , ask your doctor or pharmacist . 4 . possible side effects like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . tell your doctor or nurse straight away if you notice any of the following side effects . your doctor will give you a medicine . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .
